!Series_title	"Identification of genes involved with P. aeruginosa biofilm antibiotic resistance by microarray analysis"
!Series_geo_accession	"GSE65870"
!Series_status	"Public on May 11 2015"
!Series_submission_date	"Feb 11 2015"
!Series_last_update_date	"Jul 06 2016"
!Series_pubmed_id	"25870065"
!Series_summary	"Microarray analysis was used to identify changes in the level of transcription of genes in P. aeruginosa drip flow biofilms in response to ciprofloxacin and tobramycin exposure. This data was evaluated and used to select strains that carry transposon mutations in genes that might play a role in antibiotic tolerance of biofilms. The strains were evaluated for defects in biofilm tolerance."
!Series_overall_design	"Four drip flow biofilm conditions with three replicates each: (1) baseline controls at 72 hours, (2) tobramycin treated for 12 hours past baseline, (3) ciprofloxacin treated for 12 hrs past baseline, and (4) no treatment for 12 hrs past baseline."
!Series_type	"Expression profiling by array"

!Sample_treatment_protocol_ch1	"After 72 h of growth in the absence of antibiotic, antibiotics were added to the growth medium, and the flow with medium containing antibiotic was continued for an additional 12 h.  Tobramycin was applied at 10 μg ml-1 and ciprofloxacin at 1.0 μg ml-1." !Sample_growth_protocol_ch1	"biofilm_samples: Biofilms were formed in the continuous flow drip-flow biofilm reactor at 37 ºC using PBM supplemented with 0.2 g l-1 at a flow rate of 60 ml h-1 onto the stainless steel slides (8.5cm x 1.3cm). The reactors were inoculated by adding 1 ml of an overnight culture to 15 ml of fresh PBM to cover the slides (inoculum OD600 ≈ 0.3) in PBM (1 g l-1 glucose) for 18-24 h on a level surface. After the inoculation period, the reactor was inclined at 10º from horizontal and medium flow was initiated. The biofilms were cultured in the drip-flow reactors for 72 h (n=3) or 84 h (n=3) after the static inoculation phase for no treatment controls. After 72 h of growth in the absence of antibiotic, antibiotics were added to the growth medium, and the flow with medium containing antibiotic was continued for an additional 12 h.  Tobramycin was applied at 10 μg ml-1 and ciprofloxacin at 1.0 μg ml-1." !Sample_extract_protocol_ch1	"Cells were collected into 1ml of RNAlater® (Ambion) and stored at 4ºC for one day prior to removal of the RNAlater® by centrifugation and freezing at -70 ºC. Cells were thawed on ice and re-suspended in 300 µl of 1 mg lysozyme ml-1 in Tris-EDTA buffer, sonicated for 15 seconds, incubated at room temperature for 15 minutes, and then RNA was extracted with an RNeasy® mini kit (Qiagen Sciences) with on-column DNA digestion." !Sample_hyb_protocol	"For each Pseudomonas genome array (#900339, Affymetrix), labeled fragmented cDNA (4.5 µg from antibiotic treated biofilms, or 3 µg from planktonic cultures), was hybridized to the arrays at 50oC for 16 h with constant rotational mixing at 60 rpm.  Washing and staining of the arrays was performed using the Affymetrix GeneChip Fluidics Station 450." !Sample_data_processing	"Affymetrix CEL files were imported into FlexArray v1.6.1 for quality control, normalization, and data analysis. Microarray data was background corrected and normalized using the GC-RMA algorithm. Gene expression in 72 hour and 84 hour biofilms were pooled and compared to gene expression in antibiotic treated biofilms with an analysis of variance (ANOVA). Genes with expression changes greater than 4 fold at p ≤ 0.01 in response to ciprofloxacin or tobramycin (when compared to untreated biofilms) were selected for further analysis."	"Affymetrix CEL files were imported into FlexArray v1.6.1 for quality control, normalization, and data analysis. Microarray data was background corrected and normalized using the GC-RMA algorithm.
